                        4.2) communes should be done IN TANDEM with the neighbourhood model
                        
                        sister communes+neighbourhood in nearest city, get the benefits of both. 
                        
                        commune connected to neighbourhood  + larger network stays poly-centric, avoids most of its pitfalls.  
                        
                        a steady flow between them.
                        ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ 1716527378216649015 [2023-10-23] @octopusyarn üíú 4 üîÅ 1
                            5) I don't see the map as a one-way journey, but the establishment of a living pipeline. 
                            
                            ppl will travel along it (just like we open it up now step by step). 
                            
                            there will be many overlapping communities/psycho-geographies that exchange information 
                            
                            no single social solution https://t.co/RTHgAu0Xsx

‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ 1742495067695116459 [2024-01-03] @RichDecibels üíú 81

‚îÇ       this comes with more responsibility, more ability to mobilise resources, more commitment, more risk, more impact
‚îÇ       ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ 1742495235341512949 [2024-01-03] @RichDecibels üíú 83 üîÅ 1

‚îÇ

‚îÇ               ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ 1742495448361775293 [2024-01-03] @RichDecibels üíú 139 üîÅ 4

                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              [Quoting @RichDecibels: when you want people to take ownership of a thing you started:  *10 P's to Decentralise Leadership*  look for Person-Project-Passion fit: they need to be intrinsically motivated to contribute  the Project needs to be in Proportion: big enough to be stimulating without being overwhelming  they need an embodied sense of Permission: let them know the limits of what you trust them to handle on their own  distinguish the Principles of success, from your personal Preferences. you need to agree on Why we do things but let them figure out How  let them know the Pitfalls they are likely to encounter so they can design safe-to-fail experiments without making too big of a mess  Protect them from discouraging feedback, especially from you!  check they're making Progress: if they're accurately assessing their own performance and identifying their own learning goals, that's the best you can ask for]
